Add another 120,000 hours of our own testing and end-to-end diagnostics, and you get confidence built right in. Movement We simulated the vibrations of 1000 miles of ground transportation and jolted the Elite PCs in six directions for a total of 18 mechanical shocks. Dust Test Our Elite PCs were dusted with Arizona road dust for six hours while being operated to ensure components won't fail in harsh environments. Drop Test We made 26 drops from 30 inches onto every side, angle and edge onto 2 inches of plywood over steel and concrete to ensure toughness. Environmental We subject the Elite PCs to a simulated altitude pressure of 15,000 feet. Then, it is exposed to a temperature change of more than 212° Fahrenheit. Dedicated real-time support With HP Elite Premium Support8, you get live help desk support from a dedicated team 24x7x365 to help you tackle any challenge. It's what professional service and support should be. Standard with every Elite PC, schedule a call today, at 1-866-625-1175. Based on HP's internal analysis of mainstream business-class notebooks as of September 23, 2015 with >1 million unit annual sales having pre-installed encryption, authentication, malware protection and BIOS-level protection, passing MIL STD 810G tests, with optional docking incorporating power delivery, clamshell model, Intel Core U-Series or AMD PRO A-Series processors, built in VGA or HDMI, Display Port, RJ-45 and at least two USB 3.0 ports, integrated Smart Card reader, full connectivity offering optional WWAN, and at least 44 WHr battery. SATA drives are wiped. The remote wipe of Self Encrypting Drives that have hardware encryption active is not supported. Remote control is supported on devices with Windows 7 SP1 or higher, Windows 8, Windows 8.1 or Windows 10 (Intel®-based x86/x64) operating systems. Add another 120,000 hours of our own testing and end-to-end diagnostics, and you get confidence built right in. Movement We simulated the vibrations of 1000 miles of ground transportation and jolted the Elite PCs in six directions for a total of 18 mechanical shocks. Dust Test Our Elite PCs were dusted with Arizona road dust for six hours while being operated to ensure components won't fail in harsh environments. Drop Test We made 26 drops from 30 inches onto every side, angle and edge onto 2 inches of plywood over steel and concrete to ensure toughness. Environmental We subject the Elite PCs to a simulated altitude pressure of 15,000 feet. Then, it is exposed to a temperature change of more than 212° Fahrenheit. Dedicated real-time support With HP Elite Premium Support8, you get live help desk support from a dedicated team 24x7x365 to help you tackle any challenge. It's what professional service and support should be. Standard with every Elite PC, schedule a call today, at 1-866-625-1175. Back Features HP EliteBook 820 Sands The world's thinnest and lightest notebook in its class1 Be free of dongles and get all the ports you need to connect on the 18.9 mm ultra-slim design. Designed for productivity The HP EliteBook 820 is ready to work with the latest enterprise-class features to boost performance in and out of the office. Designed for collaboration Collaborate effectively with others using Audio by Bang & Olufsen and HP Noise Reduction Software. HP Sure Start Secure at the deepest level - HP Sure Start is the industry's first self-healing BIOS-level technology. Portable powerhouse Combine power and speed with Windows 102, latest generation Intel® Core™ processors3, a PCIe Gen3 SSD4 and DDR4 memory. Productivity anywhere you work Security Solid security Built-in security with HP Client Security, TPM, integrated HP Sure Start with Dynamic Protection and optional encrypted fingerprint reader. Manageability Easy to Manage With manageability tools like HP Touchpoint Manager5, IT can remotely manage the device over wired and wireless networks. Learn more Interactivity Simplicity of touch Pick the right display for the way you work with FHD touch display.4 Scalability Expand and upgrade Expand your system's memory, battery, storage and WWAN components.6 Productivity Accessories to meet your needs A wide variety of optional accessories like an Ultra-Slim Docking Station, displays, carrying cases, HP Notebook Power Bank providing up to eight hours of additional battery life and much more.4 Extreme tests for extreme dependability7 The HP Elite family is designed to pass MIL-STD 810G tests. Add another 120,000 hours of our own testing and end-to-end diagnostics, and you get confidence built right in. Movement We simulated the vibrations of 1000 miles of ground transportation and jolted the Elite PCs in six directions for a total of 18 mechanical shocks. Dust Test Our Elite PCs were dusted with Arizona road dust for six hours while being operated to ensure components won't fail in harsh environments. Drop Test We made 26 drops from 30 inches onto every side, angle and edge onto 2 inches of plywood over steel and concrete to ensure toughness. Environmental We subject the Elite PCs to a simulated altitude pressure of 15,000 feet. Then, it is exposed to a temperature change of more than 212° Fahrenheit. Dedicated real-time support With HP Elite Premium Support8, you get live help desk support from a dedicated team 24x7x365 to help you tackle any challenge. It's what professional service and support should be. Standard with every Elite PC, schedule a call today, at 1-866-625-1175. Based on HP's internal analysis of mainstream business-class notebooks as of September 23, 2015 with >1 million unit annual sales having pre-installed encryption, authentication, malware protection and BIOS-level protection, passing MIL STD 810G tests, with optional docking incorporating power delivery, clamshell model, Intel Core U-Series or AMD PRO A-Series processors, built in VGA or HDMI, Display Port, RJ-45 and at least two USB 3.0 ports, integrated Smart Card reader, full connectivity offering optional WWAN, and at least 44 WHr battery. Not all features are available in all editions or versions of Windows. HP Touchpoint Manager requires purchase of a subscription and supports Android™, iOS and Windows 7 or higher operating systems and PCs, notebooks, tablets and smartphones from various manufacturers. Not available in all countries see www.hp.com/touchpoint for availability information. HP Always on Remote Management features (Wipe, Lock, Unlock and reporting of BIOS boot error codes) are available on select HP EliteBooks and require an internet connection, Intel® vPro™ technology and function in S3/Sleep, S4/Hibernate and S5/Soft Off power states. SATA drives are wiped. The remote wipe of Self Encrypting Drives that have hardware encryption active is not supported. Remote control is supported on devices with Windows 7 SP1 or higher, Windows 8, Windows 8.1 or Windows 10 (Intel®-based x86/x64) operating systems. WWAN is an optional feature and use requires separately purchased service contract. Check with service provider for coverage and availability in your area. Extreme tests for extreme dependability7 The HP Elite family is designed to pass MIL-STD 810G tests. Add another 120,000 hours of our own testing and end-to-end diagnostics, and you get confidence built right in. Movement We simulated the vibrations of 1000 miles of ground transportation and jolted the Elite PCs in six directions for a total of 18 mechanical shocks. Dust Test Our Elite PCs were dusted with Arizona road dust for six hours while being operated to ensure components won't fail in harsh environments. Drop Test We made 26 drops from 30 inches onto every side, angle and edge onto 2 inches of plywood over steel and concrete to ensure toughness. Environmental We subject the Elite PCs to a simulated altitude pressure of 15,000 feet. Then, it is exposed to a temperature change of more than 212° Fahrenheit.

SATA drives are wiped. The remote wipe of Self Encrypting Drives that have hardware encryption active is not supported. Not available in all countries see www.hp.com/touchpoint for availability information. Touchpoint Manager requires purchase of a subscription. Out-of-band HP only Wipe, Lock, Unlock and reporting of BIOS boot error codes is planned to be available on select HP EliteBooks and requires an internet connection, Intel® vPro™ technology and functions in S3/Sleep, S4/Hibernate and S5/Soft Off power states. SATA drives are wiped. The remote wipe of Self Encrypting Drives that have hardware encryption active is not supported. Sold separately or as an optional feature. Elite support only available in the US and Canada in English. Not all features are available in all editions or versions of Windows. Multi-Core is designed to improve performance of certain software products. Not all customers or software applications will necessarily benefit from use of this technology. 64-bit computing system required. Performance will vary depending on your hardware and software configurations. Intel’s numbering is not a measurement of higher performance. Some functionality of this technology, such as Intel® Active management technology and Intel Virtualization technology, requires additional 3rd party software in order to run. Availability of future "virtual appliances" applications for Intel vPro technology is dependent on 3rd party software providers. Built in Qualcomm® Gobi® modules available in select HP products and require wireless data service contract, network support, and is not available in all areas. Connection speeds will vary due to location, environment, network conditions, and other factors. Availability of public wireless access points limited. The specifications for the 802.11ac WLAN are draft specifications and are not final. If the final specifications differ from the draft specifications, it may affect the ability of the notebook to communicate with other 802.11ac WLAN devices.
